\bentry
\word[O(1)]{O}
\pron{O}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
(\eng{o} eMdU \parx) (\bava\ \eng{Os} yA \eng{O's}) 
\bnum
\num{1} iMgilxSf vaNaRmAleya hadineYdaneya akaSxra. 
\hypertarget{O(1)2}{} 
\num{2} (\eng{o}) (dUravANi saMKeyx \mo\ saMKAyxsherxVNiyalilx, \kanmu\ mAtanADuvAga) sonenx; shUnayx. 
\num{3} \eng{O} vagaRda rakatx; \eng{ABO} vayxvasethxya mAnavarakatxda guMpugaLalolxMdu. 
\num{4} \eng{`o'} AkArada gurutu. 
\num{5} vatuRla; vaqtatx; \kanmu\ guMDAda AkAra. 
\enum
\emng

\num{2} (saMboVdhaneya hiMde alapxvirAma cihenxyiMda parxteyxVkisadAga \eng{o} rUpa, parxteyxVkisidAga \eng{oh} rUpa) O! OhoV! ayoyxV! ababx! \eng{O dear me}! ayoyxV nananx pADeV, goVLeV! \eng{O for a breathing-space}! O, usirADalu avakAsha sikikxdare! \eng{Oh, what a lie} ababx, eMtha suLuLx! \eng{Oh, is that so}? OhoV! hAgoV? \eng{O God}! ayoyxV deVvare!

\bentry
\word[oak(1)]{oak}
\pron{Okf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} Okf mara yA pode; kevxkaRsf kulakekx seVrida, hAlegaLaMtha elegaLuLaLx, haNuNx biDuva oMdu mara yA pode. 
\num{2} Okf (marada) dAru; \kanmu\ piVThoVpakaraNa matutx kaTaTxDagaLalilx baLasuva gaTiTxyAda, belebALuva I marada dAru. 
\num{3} (\birx) (\vivi gaLa kAleVjukoThaDigaLa) horabAgilu: \eng{sport one's oak} BeVTigAraranunx niSeVdhisalu horabAgilu hAku, mucucx. 
\hypertarget{oak(1)4}{} 
\num{4} (\eng{the Oaks}) (\Eva vAgi baLake) Okf (paMdayx); iMgelxMDina epasxmf nagaradalilx naDeyuva mUru vaSaR vayasisxna heNuNxkudure marigaLa jUju. 
\num{5} Okf (marada) elegaLu: \eng{ oak is still worn on 29th May} meV \eng{29}raMdu IgalU Okf elegaLanunx dharisalAgutatxde. 
\num{6} Okf baNaNx; Okf marada eLeyelegaLa baNaNx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum

\num{2} \eng{dyer's holm, scarlet, etc., oak} vividha jAtiya Okf maragaLu. 
\num{3} \eng{oak-beauty, oak-egger, oak-lappet, oak-hook-tip} Okf eletiMdu beLeyuva yA Okf elegaLanunx hoVluva bagebageya ciTeTxgaLu. 
\num{4} \eng{oak-fig, oak-plum, oak-potato, oak-spangle, oak-wart} Okf maragaLalilx gAlf phelxY eMba noNagaLiMda Aguva bagebageya gaMTugaLu. 
\num{5} \eng{the Oaks} = \hyperlink{oak(1)4}{$^1$oak(4)}.

\bentry

\pron{OTf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum

\banum

\banum

\num{2} \eng{off one's oats} (\AmA) hasivilalxdiru; tinanxlu iceCxyilalxdiru; AhAra beVDadiru. 
\hyperdef{O}{oat pagu(3)}{} 
\num{3} \eng{sow one's oats} (\engit{or} \eng{wild oats)} (saMyama, gAMBiVyaRgaLu sithxragoLuLxva munanx) ywvanada Baradalilx savxcaCxMdavAgi, setxYravAgi vatiRsu; ywvanadalilx gaMDAgULiyAgiru.

\bentry
\word{ob-}
\pron{abf-}
\gl{\pUparx}
\bmng
\eng{c} ge hiMde \eng{oc- (occasion)}, \eng{f} ge hiMde \eng{of (offend) p} ge hiMde \eng{op- (oppose)} rUpAMtara hoMduva, \kanmu\ lAyxTinf mUlada padagaLalilx I athaRgaLalilx parxyoVgavAguva \pUparx: 
\bnum
\num{1} goVcarate; parxkaTavAgiruvike; \eng{object, obnoxious, obtrude, obverse}. 
\num{2} edurAgu; aBumuKavAgu; edurige--kANu, iru, nilulx: \eng{observe, obvious, opportune}. 
\num{3} yAvudeV dikikxnalilx; kaDege: \eng{oblation, oblong, offer}. 
\num{4} viroVdha; devxVSa; \eng{objurgate, obloquy, obstreperous, oppose, oppress, opprobrium}. 
\num{5} parxtiroVdha; niroVdhaka; niroVdha; taDe: \eng{obdurate, obstinate, obtuse}. 
\num{6} aDiDx; aDacaNe; mare mADuvike: \eng{obese, obscure, obstacle, obstruct, occlude, occult, oppilate}. 
\num{7} aMtayx; kone; samApitx; saMpUNaRvAgiruvike: \eng{obsolete, obtain, occident, occupy}. 
\num{8} (Adhunika veYjAcnxnika pAriBASikagaLalilx) vipayaRyavAgi; parxtiloVmavAgi; vayxtirikatxvAgi; sAmAnayxvAdudakekx virudadhxvAda dikikxnalilx yA riVtiyalilx: \eng{obconical, obovate, obcordate}. 
\num{9} GaTisu; saMBavisu; saMyoVgadiMda Agu: \eng{occasion, occur, offend}. 
\num{10} namarxte; vidheVyate: \eng{obey, obsequious}. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word[objective(1)]{objective}
\pron{abfjikiTxvf}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\tashA) vAsatxva(vAda); bAhayxvasutxvina; manasisxge horagina; (jAcnxtaqvige saMbaMdhisade) jecnxVyakekx mAtarx saMbaMdhisida. 
\numi{2} (vayxkitx, leVKana, citarx, caceR, \mo vugaLa \vi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} bAhayxvasutxgaLige saMbaMdhisida; manasisxge horagaNa vasutxgaLanunx kurita. 
\alnum{b} vasutxniSaThx; vAsatxvika; vasutxBUta; idadxMtiruva; vasutxsithxtiyanunx nirUpisuva (veYyakitxka BAvagaLiMda, aBipArxyagaLiMda baNaNx kaTaTxde) vAsatxvavAda, idadxMtiruva saMgatigaLanunx tiLisuva. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{3} (\vAyx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (padada \vi) kirxyege viSayavAda. 
\alnum{b} (padada \vi) sakamaRka kirxyApadakekx kamaRpadavAda yA upasagaRdiMda niyaMtirxtavAda. 
\alnum{c} (viBakitxya \vi) divxtiVyA. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} udidxSaTx; udedxVshisida: \eng{objective point} udidxSaTx viSaya. 
\num{5} (\veYshA) (roVga lakaSxNagaLa \vi) bAhayxgoVcara; roVgiya anuBavakekx mAtarxveV oLapaTiTxrade horaginavanigU (veYdayx \mo\ vayxkitxgU) goVcaravAguva.

\banum

\numi{1} 
\banum
\alnum{a} visheVSa--GaTane, saMdaBaR; visheVSavAda yA gamanAhaRvAda--parisithxti, saMdaBaR: \eng{dressed for the occasion} saMdaBaRkekx takakxMte veVSa toTaTx; saMdaBoRVcitavAda poVSAku dharisida. \eng{on this festive occasion} I utasxva saMdaBaRdalilx. 
\alnum{b} visheVSa samaya, saMdaBaR; visheVSa saMgati yA GaTane naDeyuva nidiRSaTx samaya: \eng{on the occasion of their marriage} maduveya samayadalilx, saMdaBaRdalilx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} kAraNa; samathaRne; AdhAra: \eng{ there is no occasion to be angry} koVpisikoLaLxlu kAraNaveVnU ilalx. 
\num{3} susamaya; susaMdaBaR; sadavakAsha; yAvudeV kelasa mADalu takakx--samaya, saMdaBaR, avakAsha: \eng{take occasion} (mADalu) avakAshavanunx paDeduko, upayoVgisiko. 
\num{4} gwNa, pArxsaMgika--kAraNa; sadayxH kAraNa; tatfkaSxNada, Adare gwNavAda yA pArxsaMgikavAda kAraNa: \eng{the cause of revolution may be obscure while its occasion is obvious} kArxMtiya pArxsaMgika kAraNa sapxSaTxvAgidadxrU adara mUla kAraNavu gUDhavAgirabahudu. \eng{the assassination was the occasion of the war} KUniyu yudadhxkekx pArxsaMgika kAraNavAgitutx. 
\num{5} perxVraka (kAraNa); perxVraNe: \eng{gave occasion to a burst of laughter} goLeLxMdu nagalu kAraNavAyitu. 
\num{6} agatayx; Avashayxkate: \eng{the Queen has no occasion for the services of the officer} rANiyavarige (I) adhikAriya seVveya agatayxvilalx (avananunx vajA mADalu baLasuva swmayx sUtarx). 
\num{7} (\bava dalilx) vayxvahAragaLu; kelasakAyaRgaLu; vaqtitxge saMbaMdhisida kAyaRkalApagaLu: \eng{ go about one's lawful occasions} tananx nAyxyabadadhx vayxvahAragaLalilx niratanAgiru; tanage saMbaMdhisida kelasa kAyaRgaLanunx mADutitxru. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{celebrate the occasion} saMdaBaRvanunx utasxvarUpadalilx Acarisu. 
\num{2} \eng{rise to the occasion} asAdhAraNa saMdaBaRvodagidAga adakekx takakx yA agatayxvAda icAcxshakitx, bala, sAmathayxR, \mo vanunx toVrisu, parxdashiRsu. 
\num{3} \eng{take occasion} avakAsha baLasiko; sadavakAshavanunx upayoVgisiko. 
\numi{4} \eng{(up)on occasion} 
\banum
\alnum{a} AgAgegx; omomxmemx: Agomemx Igomemx. 
\alnum{b} agatayx bidAdxgalelalx. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\alnum{e} haDaginiMda yA vimAnadiMda KagoVLa kAyagaLa aunanxtayxvanunx aLeyuvudakAkxgi upayoVgisuva, parxtiPalana kananxDigaLa naDuve gariSaThx \eng{45} Digirx koVnavuLaLx oMdu sAdhana.

\num{3} sAmAnayxvAgi yArU gamanisada yA parigaNisada: \eng{in some odd corner} yArU gamanisada oMdu mUleyalilx. \eng{picks up odd bargains} elolxV mUleyalilxruva agagxda sarakanunx koLuLxtAtxne. 
\num{4} biDuvina; kelasavilalxda: \eng{odd moments} biDuvina, kaSxNagaLu, kAla. 
\num{5} UhisalAgada; necicxkeyilalxda; anishicxta. 
\num{6} hecicxgeya; adhika; lekakxkikxMta hecicxna: \eng{swept up the odd bits left on the floor} nelada meVle uLididadx hecicxna cUrugaLanunx guDisi etitxkoMDa. \eng{earned the odd rupee} mAmUligiMta hecicxna rUpAyiyanunx gaLisida. 
\numi{7} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\eng{3, 5} \mo vugaLaMtha saMKeyxgaLa \vi) besa; viSama; migilu; eraDu sama saMKeyxya guMpAgi viBAgisida meVle uLida yA eraDariMda nisheshxVSavAgi BAgavAgada. 
\alnum{b} (anukarxmavAgi eNike mADuvaMte joVDisiruva vasutxgaLalilx yA vayxkitxgaLalilx) besa saMKeyxya; viSama aMkeya: \eng{no parking on odd dates} besasaMKeyxya dinagaLalilx vAhanagaLa nilugaDe ilalx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} (itara elalxvanUnx vitaraNe mADida naMtara ilalxve joVDigaLAgi viBAgisida naMtarada) sheVSa; uLikeya; uLida: \eng{have got an odd sock} oMdu kAluciVla uLidide. 
\num{9} (niyata kAlikegaLu, garxMthamAle, \mo vugaLa \vi) biDi; karxmavilalxda; saMbaMdhavilalxda; oMdu sherxVNi yA oMdu vagaRdiMda beVreyAgiruva: \eng{a few odd volumes} kelavu biDi saMpuTagaLu. \eng{odd numbers} (sherxVNige karxma badadhxvAgi seVrada) biDi saMcikegaLu. 
\num{10} (saMKeyx, motatx, tUka, \mo vugaLa sUcayx padakekx seVrisidAga) -kikxMta savxlapx hecicxna; adhika cilalxreya: \eng{forty odd} nalavatUtx cilalxre; nalavatatxra meVle aivatatxroLage. \eng{sixty thousand odd} aruvatutx sAvira matutx kelavu nUrugaLu, hatutxgaLu yA biDigaLu. \eng{sixty odd thousand} aruvatutx cilalxre sAvira; aruvatutx sAvirada meVle epapxtutx sAvirada oLage. \eng{forty-odd people} nalavatutx cilalxre janagaLu; nalavatatxkikxMta hecucx, aivatatxkikxMta kaDame jana. 
\num{11} hecacxLa; uLike; meVlina cilalxreya; pUNaR saMKeyxgiMta yA hesarisida mobalagigiMta eSuTx hecocxV aSaTxra: \eng{here is a ten-rupee note; pay the bill and keep the odd money} igoV I hatutx rUpAyina noVTu tegeduko; bilalxnunx pAvati mADi uLikeyanunx, hecicxnadanunx, cilalxreyanunx niVneV iTuTxko. \eng{we have 102; what shall we do with the odd 2}? namamx hatitxra \eng{102} ide. I cilalxre eraDanunx Enu mADoVNa? 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{odd and even} sari besa yA sarimigilu ATa. 
\num{2} \eng{the odd man} besa saMKeyxya sadasayxriruva samiti \mo vugaLalilx niNARyakavAda voVTu koDuvavanu; niNARyaka matadAra. 
\numi{3} \eng{the odd man out} 
\banum
\alnum{a} nANayx miDidu mUvaralilx obabxnanunx mAtarx Ayudx koLuLxva vidhAna, upAya. 
\alnum{b} vilakaSxNa vayxkitx yA vasutx; yAvudAdaroMdu viSayadalilx oMdu taMDadalilx itara vayxkitxgaLu yA vasutxgaLigiMta beVreyAgiruva vayxkitx yA vasutx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \eng{the odd trick} (visfTx isipxVTATadalilx eraDu pakaSxgaLU ArAru paTuTxgaLanunx paDeda meVle uLida) hadimUraneya paTuTx. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word{odds}
\pron{ADf\char144}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
(\bava) 
\bnum
\num{1} (eraDU kaDegU iruva niriVkiSxta saMBAvayxteyanunx avalaMbisi, paMthagAraru oDuDxva) paNada anupAta yA adara parxmANa: \eng{give (or lay) odds of three to one} oMdakekx mUraraSuTx (paNa) oDuDx. 
\num{2} hecucx saMBava; adhika saMBAvayxte; yAvudeV pariNAma Aguva asaMBavaniVyategiMta iruva hecicxna saMBavaniVyate: \eng{the odds are that he will do it} avanu adanunx mADuva saMBavaveV hecucx: \eng{the odds are that it will rain} maLeyAguva saMBavaveV hecucx. 
\num{3} parxtikUlakikxMta hecicxna anukUla; \eng{the odds are in oue favour} namage parxtikUlaveV hecAcxgide. \eng{I have fought against longer odds} idakikxMta hecicxna parxtikUlagaLanunx edurisidedxVne (eMdare Iga parxtikUla aSeTxVnU hecicxlalx), \eng{won the against all the adds} elalx parxtikUlagaLidadxrU, elalx parxtikUlagaLa virudadhx gedadx. \eng{the adds are against him} avanu gelulxva sAdhayxte kaDame. 
\num{4} (sapxdhiRgaLalilx dubaRlanAdavanige itararoDane sama avakAsha kalipxsikoDalu niVDuva) riyAyiti: \eng{give adds}(dubaRla sapxdhiRge) riyAyiti niVDi samAvakAsha kalipxsikoDu. 
\num{5} (anukUlakara) vayxtAyxsa: \eng{what is the adds}? adariMdeVnu? adariMdeVnu toMdare? \eng{it makes no adds} adariMda EnU vayxtAyxsavAgadu. 
\num{6} (\pArxparx) hecucxkaDame; veYSamayx; asamate: \eng{make adds even} hecucx kaDime ilalxdaMte mADu; sarisama mADu. 
\num{7} viroVdha; hoVrATa; parxtikUla: \eng{they are at adds with fate} avaru vidhiyoDane, adaqSaTxdoDane hoVrADutitxdAdxre.

\bentry
\word[off(1)]{off}

\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} dUra; dUrakekx; dUradalilx: \eng{ward off disaster} vipatatxnunx dUra mADu. \eng{drove off} dUra ODisida. \eng{is three miles off} mUru meYli dUradalilxde. 
\numi{2} 
\banum
\alnum{a} nele tapipx; sAthxnabiTuTx; seVrirade; soVkirade; saMbaMdhisirade: \eng{my hat is off} nananx hAyxTanunx taleyiMda tegedide. \eng{has come off} biTuTx hoVgide; kitutx hoVgide; hora baMdide. 
\alnum{b} kaLaci, bicicx (hAki): \eng{take his clothes off} avana baTeTxyanunx kaLaci hAku: \eng{take your coat off} ninanx koVTanunx kaLaci hAku. 
\eanum

\bentry
\word[oil(1)]{oil}
\pron{Ailf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} eNeNx; teYla; niVrinalilx karagada, niVrina meVle teVluva, AlakxhAlf, Itharf, beni\char144Vnf, \mo\ kAbaRnika dArxvakagaLalilx karaguva, jiDuDx savxBAvada, rAsAyanikavAgi taTasathx guNada, uriyabalalx darxva padAthaR yA sulaBavAgi darxvavAguva Gana padAthaR. 
\num{2} (\ame) = \hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{petroleum}{petroleum}. 
\num{3} (\saMpa gaLalilx) iMdhana; iMdhanavAgi baLasuva eNeNx: \eng{oil-lamp} eNeNxdiVpa. 
\numi{4} (\sA\ \bava dalilx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} = \hyperlink{oil-paint}{oil-paint}. 
\alnum{b} (\AmA) teYla vaNaRcitarx; teYla vaNaRcitarxgaLanunx baLasi racisida citarx: \eng{his best oils are exhibited here} ililx Atana atuyxtatxma teYla vaNaRcitarxgaLanunx parxdashiRsalAgide. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{5} (\bava dalilx) = \hyperlink{oilskin}{oilskin}. 
\num{6} beNeNxmAtu; muKasutxti mADuva, pusalAyisuva mAtu. 
\numi{7} (\AseTxrXV\ matutx nUyxsizVlaMDf) 
\banum

\alnum{b} saMgatigaLu; nijAMshagaLu. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\hyperdef{O}{oil(1) pagu(1)}{} 
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{burn the midnight oil} rAtirx bahaLa hotitxnavaregU Odu yA kelasa mADu. 
\num{2} \eng{drying oil} Aruva eNeNx; oNaguva eNeNx; gALigoDiDxdAga oNaguva eNeNx; vAyuvina kirxyeyiMda gaTiTxyAguva, AdudariMda oNagidaMtAguva, kelavu bageya biVjagaLiMda tegeda AviyAguvaMthadalalxda yAvudeV eNeNx, \udA\ agase eNeNx. 
\num{3} \eng{non-drying oil} Arada eNeNx; Ganisada eNeNx; vAyuvina kirxyeyiMda gaTiTxyAgada yAvudeV kobebxNeNx. 
\num{4} \eng{oil and vinegar} (\engit{or} \eng{water)} eNeNx siVgekAyi; parasapxra virudadhxvAdavu. 
\num{5} \eng{oil of almonds} bAdAmi eNeNx; bAdAmi biVjadiMda tegeda eNeNx. 
\num{6} \eng{oil of vitriol} = \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{sulphuric acid}{sulphuric acid}. 
\num{7} \eng{pour oil on the flame} uriyuva beMkige tupapx suri; parisithxtiyanunx ulabxNisu. 
\num{8} \eng{pour oil on the water} shamana mADu; samAdhAna mADu; sAMtavxnagoLisu. 
\num{9} \eng{salad oil} salADf eNeNx; salADf tayArisalu baLasuva eLeLxNeNxyaMtha yAvudeV eNeNx. 
\num{10} \eng{show smell of oil} (parxtiBegiMta hecAcxgi) sharxmada yA duDimeya cihenx toVru. 
\num{11} \eng{strap oil} beliTxniMda bArisu, hoDe. 
\numi{12} \eng{strike oil} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (eNeNxgAgi bAvi koredAga sudeYvadiMda) eNeNx paDe. 
\alnum{b} adaqSaTxshAliyAgi aishavxyaRgaLisu, yashasusx paDe.

\bentry
\word[olive(1)]{olive}
\pron{Alivf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
Alivf: 
\hypertarget{olive(1)a}{} 
\banum
\alnum{a} Alivf mara; Oliya kulakekx seVrida, kaDuhasiru baNaNxda BalelxyAkArada togalinaMtidudx, keLaBAgadalilx biLupAgiruva elegaLuLaLx, \kanmu\ meDiTareVniyanf parxdeVshada Aliya yUroVpiya matutx dakiSxNa Aphirxkada Aliya AphirxkAna kulagaLige seVrida, nitayx haridavxNaRda yAvudeV mara. \imglink{\(^1\)olive a.:fig}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage width 0.5cm height 0.5cm {O_Pictures/olive-a.jpg}}} 
\alnum{b} Alivf haNuNx; gaDusAda biVja matutx adanAnxvarisida maqduvAda kahi tiruLiruva haNuNx biDuva, mAgilalxdAga hasurAgiyU mAgida meVle niVli kapupx baNaNxdAdxgiyU iruva, aMDAkArada cikakx haNuNx. 
\hypertarget{olive(1)c}{} 
\alnum{c} Alivf baNaNx; pakavxvAgada Alivf haNiNxna nasu bUdu hasuru baNaNx. 
\hypertarget{olive(1)d}{} 
\alnum{d} Alivf (marada) dAru. 
\alnum{e} (\aMrashA) Alivf Utaka; himimxduLina (\eng{medula oblongata})lilxruva Alivf kAyiya AkArada ububx gubuTugaLeraDaralilx oMdu. 
\alnum{f} (\pArxvi) Aliva kulakekx seVrida, alivf haNiNxna AkArada udarapadi maqdavxMgi yA I maqdavxMgiya cipupx. 
\alnum{g} (danada yA karuvina) mAMsada cUru \mo vugaLanunx Alivf kAyina AkAradalilx suruLi mADi beVyisida BakaSxyX. 
\alnum{h} (shAMti saMdhAna sUcakavAgi) Alivf--ele, koMbe , elegaLa daMDe. 
\hypertarget{olive(1)i}{} 
\alnum{i} Alivf kAyina AkArada (adakekx javAbAda inonxMdu kuNikeyoLakekx hAki uDupanunx BadarxpaDisuva) guMDi \mo\ sAdhana.

\num{3} muMdakekx; inUnx muMdakekx; agarxsAthxnadalilx; muMduvarida sAthxnadalilx yA sithxtiyalilx: \eng{time is getting on} kAla muMde muMde hoVgutitxde. \eng{it happened later on} adu AmeVle naDeyitu.

\bnum

\num{2} AgatAneV; AgaSeTxV; Aga mAtarx; hiMde Agirade: \eng{saw them only yesterday} avaranunx keVvala ninenx noVDide, ninenxyaSeTxV noVDide (hiMde alalx). 
\num{3} alilxyavarege, muMce--alalxde; -neV; -veV: \eng{arrives only on Tuesday} maMgaLavAraveV baruvudu (adakekx muMce alalx).

\noindent

\num{3} \eng{only too} bahaLa; ati; tiVra: \eng{only too glad} (niriVkiSxsidadxkekx yA iciCxsidadxkekx vayxtirikatxvAgi) bahaLa saMtoVSa. \eng{only too true} tiVra nija.

\word[open(1)]{open}
\pron{Opanf}
\gl{\gu}
\expl{(\tara\ \eng{opener}, \tama\ \eng{openest}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} tereda; terapiruva; mukatx; mucicxlalxda; taDegaTiTxlalxda; KulAlx; parxveVshakekx, saMcArakekx yA hAdige--avakAshaviruva: \eng{open passage} mukatx, tereda--mAgaR. 
\num{2} (koThaDi, meYdAna yA itara parxdeVsha) terediruva; mukatx; AvaraNavilalxda; sututxgaTiTxlalxda; taDeyilalxda; aDiDxyilalxda: \eng{the open road} mukatxvAda rasetx. 
\num{3} (Dababx, dhAraka, \mo vugaLa \vi) mucicxlalxda; terediruva; mucacxLa hAkada. 
\num{4} tereda; mare tegediruva; mucicxlalxda; anAvaqta: \eng{open carriage} cAvaNiyilalxda baMDi; boVLugADi. \eng{open drain} tereda caraMDi. \eng{open wound} (paTiTx \mo vugaLiMda) mucicxlalxda gAya. 
\num{5} (ATa) (goVlina bAyi yA itara AkarxmaNada vasutxvina \vi) arakiSxta; AkarxmaNakekx tutAtxguva. 
\num{6} mucucxmareyilalxda; parxkaTa; bahiraMga: \eng{open contempt} bahiraMga tirasAkxra. \eng{open scandal} bahiraMga pukAru. \eng{open hostilities} parxkaTa hoVrATagaLu, kadanagaLu. 
\num{7} tereda; bicicxda; haraDida; haraDikoMDiruva; haraDiruva: \eng{open book} tereda pusatxka. \eng{had the map open on the table} meVjina meVle BUpaTavanunx terediTiTxdadx, bicicxTaTx. 
\num{8} (baTeTxya \vi) otAtxgilalxda, jALAgiruva; naDuve aMtaragaLiruva. 
\num{9} (vayxkitxya \vi) mucucxmareyilalxde; bicucx manasisxna; saraLa haqdayada; tereda manasisxna; BAvanegaLanunx itararige tiLisabayasuva.

\num{13} (saBeya \vi) mukatx; sAvaRjanika; savaRrigU parxveVshaviruva; elalxrigU parxveVshAvakAshaviruva; keVvala sadasayxrU \mo varige siVmitavAgirade elalxrU barabahudAda.

\bentry
\word{opinion}
\pron{Apinayxnf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} aBipArxya: \eng{in my opinion} nananx aBipArxyadalilx; nanage toVruvudaralilx. 
\num{2} sadayxda naMbike: \eng{am of opinion that} I riVtiyAgi sadayxdalilx naMbidedxVne. 
\num{3} eNike; toVcike; anisike. 
\num{4} janABipArxya; loVkABipArxya; loVkamata; janasAmAnayxralilx rUDhiyAgiruva, (\kanmu\ neYtika parxshenxgaLanunx kurita) BAvane yA aBipArxya. 
\num{5} (nidiRSaTx parxshenxya bagegx obabxna) AloVcane; daqDhABipArxya; daqDha naMbike: \eng{my opinion on smoking} dhUmapAnada bagegx nananx aBipArxya, AloVcane. 
\num{6} (vAsatxvAMsha yA sariyAda karxma hiVgeMdu salahe keVLidAga niVDuva) tajAcnxBipArxya; tajacnx salahe; tajacnxna, pariNatana--vidhivatAtxda heVLike; vaqtitx nipuNana aBipArxya: \eng{you had better have another opinion} niVnu matotxbabx tajacnxna salaheyanunx paDeyuvudu meVlu. 
\num{7} eNike; aBipArxya: \eng{have a very high opinion of him} avana bagegx nanage bahaLa oLeLxya aBipArxyavide. 
\num{8} (niSeVdhapadadoDane) sadaBipArxya; oLeLxya aBipArxya; mecicxke toVrisuva aBipArxya: \eng{I have no opinion of Frenchmen} pherxMcf janara bagegx nanage oLeLxya aBipArxyavilalx. 
\num{9} (\nAyxshA) kAraNa--nideRVsha, nirUpaNa; tiVpiRge AdhAravAda kAraNagaLanunx tiLisuva viduyxkatx heVLike. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{act up to one's opinions} tananx daqDhABipArxyagaLige anusAravAgi naDe. 
\num{2} \eng{a matter of opinion} aBipArxyada, BinAnxBipArxyada viSaya. 
\num{3} \eng{be of the opinion} hAgeMdu aBipArxyapaDu, naMbu. 
\num{4} \eng{in one's opinion} obabxna aBipArxyadalilx, naMbikeyalilx. 
\num{5} \eng{the courage of one's opinions} aBipArxya dheYyaR; tananx daqDhanaMbikegaLaMte naDeyuva dheYyaR. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[order(1)]{order}
\pron{ADaRrf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} sherxVNi; soVpAna; sAlu; paMkitx (Iga \viparx): \eng{order on order of sculptured figures} sherxVNiya meVle sherxVNiyAgidadx shilapxkaqtigaLu. 
\num{2} sAmAjika vagaR, dajeR, aMtasutx: \eng{the higher orders} meVladxjeRgaLu. 
\num{3} bage; taraha; parxkAra; riVti: \eng{talents of a high order} unanxta maTaTxda sahaja shakitxgaLu. 
\num{4} (deVvatA)vagaR; `serAphimf', `cerubimf', \mo\ oMbatutx vagaRda deVvategaLalilx yAvudeV vagaR. 
\num{5} (kerxYsatx pAdirxgaLa) vagaR; sherxVNi; dajeR; biSapf, DiVkanf, \mo\ beVre beVre dajeRgaLalilx oMdu: \eng{(holy) orders} pAdirx padavi, hudedx. 
\num{6} (mAMkfgaLu, pharxyarfgaLu matutx hiMde (kerxYsatx) dhamaRviVraru, meVsanaru, \mo vara) vagaR; daLa; paMtha: \eng{Franciscan order} saMta phAnisxsasxna vagaR, daLa, paMtha. 
\numi{7} (rAjaniMda birudu \mo vugaLanunx paDedu sanAmxtitarAdavara) 
\banum
\alnum{a} vagaR; sherxVNi: \eng{Order of the Garter} gATaRrf vagaR. 
\alnum{b} iMtha vagaRdavara lAMCana: \eng{wears the order of the Golden Fleece} `goVlaDxnf philxVSf' vagaRda lAMCanavanunx dharisutAtxne. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} (\vAshi) riVti; sheYli: \eng{five (classical) orders} aidu aBijAta sheYligaLu (DoVrikf, ayAnikf, koriMtiyanf, Tasakxnf matutx kAMposiTf). \imglink{\(^1\)orders 8.:fig}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage width 0.6cm height 0.4cm {O_Pictures/orders-8.jpg}}} 
\numi{9} (\ga) dajeR: 
\banum
\alnum{a} yAvudeV biVjagaNitoVkitxyalilxruva padagaLalilx kANabaruva atuyxnanxta GAta: \eng{$\left(ax^2+bx+c\right)$} \eng{is an equation of the second order}. \eng{$\left(ax^2+bx+c\right)$} eMbudu eraDane dajeRya gaNitoVkitx. 
\alnum{b} (yAvudeV motatxda parxmANavanunx nideRVshisuva) dajeR; maTaTx: \eng{the wavelength of visible light is of the order of thousand angstroms} daqshayx beLakina aleyudadx halavu sAvira AYxMgfsATxrXmfgaLa dajeRyadu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{10} (\jiVvi) gaNa; pArxNigaLa vagiRVkaraNadalilx vagaRkikxMta keLaginadu matutx vaMshakikxMta meVlinadu. 
\num{11} (\sA\ \eng{10}ra guNada, gAtarxda AdhArada meVle vagiRVkarisida padadhxti yA vayxvasethxyalilxna) vagaR: \eng{order of magnitude} gAtarxda AdhArada meVle, \sA\ \eng{10}ra GAtada AdhArada meVle, vagiRVkarisalAguva padadhxtiya oMdu vagaR. 
\num{12} karxma; anukarxma: \eng{alphabetical order} akArAdi karxma. 
\num{13} vayxvasithxta karxma; vayxvasethx; parxtiyoMdu aMsha, BAga, \mo vu tamamx ucita sAthxnadalilxruva sithxti: \eng{love of order} (utatxma) vayxvasethxya perxVma. 
\num{14} (\birx) (\pArxparx) kAyaRkarxma; vidhAna: \eng{take order to do} (yAvudanenxV) mADalu (agatayxvAda) kAyaRkarxmavanunx anusarisu. 
\num{15} jagatutx, samAja, \mo vugaLa savxrUpa yA vayxvasethx, karxma: \eng{the moral order of the world} jagatitxna neYtika vayxvasethx. 
\num{16} (shAsanasaBe \mo vugaLalilx anusarisabeVkAda niyamAvaLigaLu, kAyaRvidhAna, \mo vugaLa) shisutx; karxma; paripATa; riVti: \eng{Order}! \eng{Order}! shisutx! shisutx!. 
\num{17} shAMtivayxvasethx; shAMti (parisithxti); galaBe, goMdalagaLu ilalxde, kAnUnugaLanunx pAlane mADutatx iruva sithxti: \eng{law and order} shAMta sithxti; shAsana badadhx vayxvasethx; shAMti: \eng{law and order was restored} shAMtiyanunx punaH sAthxpisalAyitu. \eng{keep order} shAMti (sithxti) pAlisi. 
\num{18} (seYnayx) sAlu; paMkitx; sherxVNi; seYnikaranunx joVDisiruva karxma: \eng{open order} tereda sAlu; viraLa sAlu; seYnika--seYnikara naDuve aMtaraviruvaMte nililxsida seYnikara sAlu. \eng{close order} mucicxda sAlu; otutx sAlu; seYnikarelalx otAtxgi, naDuve aMtara ilalxde nilulxva sAlu. 
\num{19} (\bava dalilx saha) kaTuTxpADu; kaTaTxLe; apapxNe; Ajecnx; AdeVsha; hukumu: \eng{gave orders} apapxNe, --koTaTx. \eng{till further orders} muMdina AdeVshadavarege. 
\num{20} (bAyxMkiMgf \mo vugaLa) nideRVsha; sUcane. 
\numi{21} (vANijayx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} koVrike; nideRVsha; sUcane; ADaRru; vAyxpArigoV tayArakanigoV yAvudeV sarakanunx sarabarAju mADuvaMte kaLuhisida sUcane. 
\alnum{b} hAge odagisida saraku \mo vugaLa motatx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{22} (nATaka yA saMgiVta shAle, mUyxsiyamf, KAsagi mane, \mo vugaLige shulakxrahitavAgi yA alapx shulakxkekx yA oMdu hakAkxgi, parxveVshisalu koDuva) parxveVshapatarx; apapxNe ciVTi; pAsu. 
\num{23} (\kerxY) dhAmiRka vidhi; vidhuyxkatxvAda kamaRvidhAna: \eng{the order of confirmation} (jAcnxnasAnxnavAdavarige niVDuva) sithxriVkaraNa saMsAkxra vidhi. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{a large order} (\AmA) kaSaTxvAda kelasa; duSakxra kAyaR. 
\num{2} \eng{by order} (adhikaqta adhikAriya) apapxNeya parxkAra; AjAcnxnusAra. 
\num{3} \eng{call to order} (ceVrfmananxna \vi) (saBeyu) AraMBavAyiteMdu GoVSisu. 
\num{4} \eng{holy orders} (AYxMgilxkanf caciRna) dhAmiRka sAthxnagaLu; biSapf, pirxVsfTx matutx DiVkanf eMba dajeRgaLu. 
\num{5} \eng{in bad order} sariyAgi kelasa mADutitxlalxda; keTiTxruva. 
\num{6} \eng{in (good) order} sariyAda vayxvasethx iruva; susithxtiyalilxruva; cenAnxgi kelasa mADuvaMtiruva; baLasuva sithxtiyalilxruva. 
\num{7} \eng{in (holy) orders} diVkeSx paDedu; diVkiSxtanAgi. 
\num{8} \eng{in order} karxmabadadhxvAgiruva. 
\hypertarget{orderpagu9}{} 
\num{9} \eng{in order that} udedxVshadiMda; (yAvudanenxV) mADalu, mADuvudakAkxgi, mADuvudakokxVsakxra, mADuva saluvAgi. 
\num{10} \eng{in order to} = \hyperlink{orderpagu9}{?pagu?\((9)\)}. 
\hypertarget{order1pagu11}{} 
\numi{11} \eng{in the order of} 
\banum
\alnum{a} sumArAgi; aMdAjinalilx. 
\alnum{b} heVLiruva, sUcisiruva--parxmANadalilx, gAtarxdalilx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{12} \eng{in working order} (sariyAgi) kelasa mADutitxruva; susithxtiyalilxruva. 
\num{13} \eng{keep order} shisutx sAthxpisu; karxmabadadhxvAda naDavaLikeyanunx anusarisuvaMte mADu. 
\hyperdef{O}{order(1) pagu(14)}{} 
\numi{14} \eng{made to order} 
\banum
\alnum{a} nideRVshadaMte mADida; heVLidaMte mADida. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) apeVkiSxta; apeVkiSxsiruvudakekx sariyAgiruva, takukxdAgiruva. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{15} \eng{minor orders} (\roVkAyx\ caciRna) sAmAnayx sAthxnagaLu; DiVkanf eMbudakikxMta keLagina dajeRgaLu. 
\num{16} \eng{money order} (haNavanunx viLAsadAranige koDuvaMte aMce kaceVriya koDuva, beVrobabxrige vagARyisalAgada) maniADaRru. 
\num{17} \eng{not in order} = \hyperlink{order1pagu26}{?pagu?\((26)\)}. 
\num{18} \eng{of the order of} = \hyperlink{order1pagu11}{?pagu?\((11)\)}. 
\num{19} \eng{on order} (sarakugaLa \vi) koVrida; kaLuhisuvaMte AdeVsha koTiTxruva, Adare inUnx paDedilalxda. 
\num{20} \eng{on the order of} = \hyperlink{order1pagu11}{?pagu?\((11)\)}. 
\num{21} \eng{order cheque} ADaRrf cekukx; haNa paDeyuvavanu haNa paDeyuva modalu ruju mADikoDabeVkAda cekukx. 
\num{22} \eng{Order in Council} (\birx) pirxvi kwnisxlilxna salaheya meVrege yAvudeV ADaLitada viSayadalilx rAjanu mADuva rAjAjecnx. 
\num{23} \eng{Order of the} \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{bath(1) pagu}{$^1$bath}. 
\hyperdef{O}{order(1)24}{} 
\numi{24} \eng{order of the day} 
\banum
\alnum{a} dinada kAyaRkarxma; naDesalu gotutxpaDisiruva kelasa. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) sadayxda sithxti; iMdina, vataRmAna parisithxti; parxcalita vidayxmAna: \eng{cricket is the order of the day} kirxkeTf ATa Igina, iMdina, cAlitx SoVki Agide. 
\alnum{c} (\rUpa) keYgoLaLxbeVkAda kAyaRda muKayx vicAra. 
\alnum{d} nidhARrita kAyaRkarxma; gotutx paDisida, tiVmARnisida--kAyaRvidhAna. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{25} \eng{order to view} girAkiyu kaTaTxDavanunx pariVkiSxsalu mane daLALxLiya koVrike. 
\hypertarget{order1pagu26}{} 
\num{26} \eng{out of order} vayxvasethx keTiTxruva; sariyAgi kelasa mADutitxlalxda. 
\hypertarget{order1pagu27}{} 
\num{27} \eng{postal order} (\birx) (haNavanunx viLAsadAranige koDuvaMte aMce kaceVriyu koDuva, beVrobabxrige vagARyisalAgada) aMceADaRru. 
\num{28} \eng{post-office order} = \hyperlink{order1pagu27}{?pagu?\((27)\)}. 
\num{29} \eng{review order} parxdashaRna kAladalilx seYnikaru dharisabeVkAda uDupu matutx shasatxrXgaLu. 
\num{30} \eng{rise to a point of order} = \hyperlink{order1pagu31}{?pagu?\((31)\)}. 
\hypertarget{order1pagu31}{} 
\num{31} \eng{rise to order} (niyamAvaLiya parxkAra) karxmabadadhxteyanunx parxshinxsalu ELu. 
\hypertarget{order1pagu32}{} 
\num{32} \eng{take holy orders} pAdirxya diVkeSx paDe. 
\hyperdef{O}{order(1) pagu(33)}{} 
\numi{33} \eng{take orders} 
\banum
\alnum{a} AdeVshagaLanunx, nirUpagaLanunx--opipx kAyaRrUpakekx taru, kAyaRgatagoLisu. 
\alnum{b} AdeVshagaLanunx paDe; AjecnxgaLanunx sivxVkarisu.

\eanum

\num{1} (\shavi) deYhika; AMgika; Avayavika; aMgAMgagaLa, avakekx saMbaMdhisida: \eng{organic changes caused by emotion} BAvoVderxVkadiMda uMTAda deYhika badalAvaNegaLu.

\banum

\alnum{b} vayxvasithxtavAda aMgagaLiMda racitavAda; avayava GaTita; AMgika; Avayavika: \eng{organic structure of animals and plants} sasayx matutx pArxNigaLa AMgika, Avayavika racane. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} (\roVshA) (vAyxdhiya \vi) aMgavikaqta; AMgika vayxtAyxsajanayx; aMgavikaqtijanayx; aMgada racaneyalAlxgiruva badalAvaNeyiMduMTAda.

\banum

\alnum{b} (kaqSi) rAsAyanika gobabxra, kiVTanAshaka, \mo vanunx baLasade beLeda, utApxdisida: \eng{organic farming} jeYvika kaqSi. \eng{organic manure} jeYvika gobabxra.

\eanum

\banum

\bentry
\word{orthodox}
\pron{AtaRDAkfsx}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} sAMparxdAyika: 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\kanmu\ dhAmiRka tatatxvX, niVti, \mo\ viSayagaLalilx) sariyAda yA vADikeyalilxruva aBipArxyagaLanunx hoMdiruva. 
\alnum{b} savxtaMtarxciMtaneyadalalxda; savxMtadadxlalxda; hosadalalxda. 
\alnum{c} dhamaRvirudadhx yA shAsatxrX virudadhxvAgilalxda; yathAshAsitxrXVya; shAsAtxrXnusAriyAda. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (dhAmiRka sidAdhxMta, neYtika mAnadaMDa, \mo vugaLa \vi) sAMparxdAyika; shAsitxrXVya; sari athavA satayx eMdu sAmAnayxvAgi opipxruva, aMgiVkarisiruva; shAsitxrXVyavAgi, adhikaqtavAgi--sAthxpitavAda, aMgiVkaqtavAda.

\emng

\bentry
\word[other(1)]{other}
\pron{adarf}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} beVrobabx yA beVroMdu; inonxMdu yA inonxbabx; matotxMdu yA matotxbabx; anayx; itara; para; beVre; IgAgaleV heVLidadxlalxda yA sUcisidadxlalxda; vayxkitx yA jAtiyalilx BinanxvAda: \eng{other people} beVreyavaru; itara jana. \eng{other means} beVre sAdhana; Binanx mAgaR. \eng{my reason is quite other} nananx kAraNa tiVra beVreyAdudu. 
\num{2} adhika; hecicxna; beVre; matetx; jotege: \eng{we have other evidence} namamxlilx beVre (hecicxna) sAkaSxyXvide. \eng{a few other examples} matetx kelavu udAharaNegaLu. 
\num{3} eraDaralilx oMdu yA ibabxralilx obabx: \eng{open your other eye} ninanx inonxMdu kaNuNx tere. 
\num{4} (\eng{the} oDane) uLida; mikakx; parxsakatxvAdudanunx biTuTx itara elalxvanUnx parigaNisida, nirAkarisida, \mo\ taruvAya uLiyuva: \eng{must be in the other pocket} inonxMdu jiVbinalilxrabeVku. \eng{where are the other two}? uLidibabxru yA mikikxbabxru elilx? 
\num{5} (\eng{than} jotege) vinA; biTuTx; horatu; uLidu: \eng{any person other than you} ninanxnunx biTuTx yAvanAdarU. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{an other two} 
\banum
\alnum{a} beVre eraDu. 
\alnum{b} matetx eraDu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{every other day} dinabiTuTx dina; parxti marudina: \eng{happens every other day} parxti marudina saMBavisutatxde. 
\num{3} \eng{no} (\engit{or} \eng{none) other than} beVre yArU yA yAvudU alalx: \eng{it was none other than Ram} adu beVre yArU Agirade, savxyaM rAmaneV Agidadx. 
\num{4} \eng{on the other hand} (hiMdinadakekx virudadhxvAda yA vayxtAyxsavAda saMgatiyanunx yA vAdavanunx muMdiDuvAga \parx) sariyAgi noVDidare; inonxMdu kaDeyalilx; matotxMdu saMdaBaR yoVcisidare. 
\num{5} \eng{other things being equal} mikakx viSayagaLu samavAgidudx yA samavAgidadxre. 
\num{6} \eng{somehow or other} heVgoV; heVgAdarU; yAvudeV riVtiyalilx. 
\num{7} \eng{some one or other} yArAdarU; yAvanAdarU obabx: \eng{some idiots or other have been shouting all night hoarse} yAroV aviveVkigaLu rAtirxyelAlx bobebx hAkutitxdadxru. 
\num{8} \eng{something or other} yAvudAdarU oMdu. 
\num{9} \eng{some time or other} eMdAdarU, oMdalalx oMdu dina. 
\num{10} \eng{some way or other} yAvudAdarU, yAvudoV oMdu -- riVtiyalilx. 
\num{11} \eng{the other thing} (\kanmu\ hAsayx \parx) (sapxSaTxvAgi adanunx heVLadiruvAga) A inonxMdu: \eng{if you don't like it, do the other thing} ninage adu hiDisadidadxre, A inonxMdanunx mADu. 
\num{12} \eng{the other day}(\engit{or} \eng{night or week etc.,)} aMdu; Avatutx; kelavu dinagaLa hiMde; ititxVcege; monenxmonenx. 
\num{13} \eng{the other two} (anidiRSaTxvAgi heVLuvAga \parx) mikikxbabxru; uLideraDu. 
\num{14} \eng{the other woman} A inonxbabx heMgasu; vivAhitana upapatinx, nalelx. 
\num{15} \eng{the other world} paraloVka. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[out(1)]{out}
\pron{auTf}
\gl{\kirxvi}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} horage; horagaDe; Ace; horakekx; horagaDege; Acege: \eng{he is out} avanu (maneyiMda) horage hoVgidAdxne. \eng{keep him out} avananunx horagiDu. \eng{turn him out} avananunx horakekx aTuTx. \eng{get out of here} ililxMda horakekx hoVgu. \eng{my son is out in Canada} nananx maga kenaDAdalilx idAdxne. 
\numi{2} (\pagu da \kirx gaLanunx rUpisuvAga) 
\banum
\alnum{a} oMdu sathxLa \mo vugaLiMda cedari hoVguvudanunx sUcisuvalilx: \eng{hire out } bADigege tegedukoMDu hoVgu. \eng{board out} beVre kaDe hoVgi UTa mADu. 
\alnum{b} sAvaRjanikara gamana \mo vugaLige baruvudu yA taruvudanunx sUcisalu: \eng{call out} \eng{(i)} kUgu; GoVSisu. \eng{(ii)} kUgi kare. \eng{(iii)} lakaSxyXviDabeVkAda Avashayxkateyanunx sUcisalu: \eng{watch out} gamanisu. \eng{look out} noVDu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} horage; horagaDe; mane, kaceVri, \mo\ kaDegaLalilx ilalxde: \eng{went out for a walk} horagaDe naDagege hoVdaru. \eng{she has her Sundays out} avaLu BAnuvAragaLanunx maneyiMda horage kaLeyutAtxLe. 
\num{4} pUNaRvAgi; pUtiR(yAgi); mugiyuvavarege; konetanaka: \eng{she had her cry out} Ake (tananx duHKavelalx mugiyuvavaregU) pUtiRyAgi atutx biTaTxLu, aLuvaSuTx atutx mugisidaLu. \eng{tried out} (shakitxyelalx mugidu hoVguvaSuTx) pUtiR AyAsavAgiru; basavaLidiru; susAtxgi hoVgiru. \eng{die out} pUtiR aLidu hoVgu. \eng{fight it out} kone tanaka hoVrADu. \eng{typed it out} pUtiR beraLacucx mADida. 
\num{5} (beMki, moVMbatitx, \mo vugaLa \vi) Ari; naMdi; uriyade. 
\num{6} (lekAkxcAra, aMdAju, niriVkaSxNe) tapATxgi: \eng{I was out in my calculations} nananx lekAkxcAravelalx, niriVkaSxNeyelalx tapApxgi hoVyitu. 
\num{7} (\AmA) parxjecnxyilalxde; mUCeR hoVgi; jAcnxna tapipx: \eng{she was out for five minutes} avaLu aidu nimiSa mUCeR hoVgidadxLu. 
\numi{8} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (halilxna \vi) kitutx; tegedu hAki. 
\alnum{b} (kiVlu, mULe, \mo vugaLa \vi) kiVlu tapipx; sAthxna palalxTavAgi: \eng{his arm is out} avana toVLu kiVlu tapipx hoVgide. \eng{put his shoulder out} Buja sAthxnapalalxTavAyitu. 
\eanum
\numie

\bentry
\word[over(1)]{over}
\pron{Ovarf}
\gl{\kirxvi}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (oMdara) meVliMda; Acege; keLakekx: \eng{lean over} (doNeNx, meVju, \mo vugaLa) meVle--oragu, Anu yA bAgiko. \eng{fall over} (oMdara) meVle biVLu. \eng{knock over} (oMdara) meVle hoDedu, baDidu--keDavu, uruLisu. \eng{jump over} (goVDe \mo vugaLa) meVliMda (Acege) nege, hAru, laMGisu. 
\num{2} meVlemxY meVle; meYmeVlelalx; iDiV meYmeVle; iDiV meVlemxYyanunx mucucxvaMte: \eng{brush it over} (meY, aMgi, \mo vanunx) pUtiRyAgi oresu, barxSf mADu. \eng{paint it over} oMdara meYmeVle baLi, savaru, leVpisu. 
\num{3} (oMdanunx dATikoMDu) meVle; meVlakekx; meVleDege: \eng{climb over} (oMdara) meVle--Eru, hatutx, aDaru. \eng{look over} (hegalu \mo vugaLa) meVliMda bAgi, iNuki--noVDu. 
\num{4} (maDicalu, hiMdirugisalu yA talekeLagu mADalu) meVle yA hiMdakekx yA talekeLagAgi: \eng{bend it over} (adanunx oMdara) meVle bagigxsu, bAgisu. \eng{fold it over} hiMdakekx maDicu. \eng{turn over} (hALeyanunx) hiMdakekx tirugisu, magucu, tiruvihAku. 
\num{5} (pakakxgaLanunx, tudigaLanunx badalAyisalu kirxkeTf aMpeYrf koDuva sUcane) Ovarf! Ayitu! mugiyitu! (I kaDeyadu mugiyitu, A kaDeyadanunx AraMBisabeVku eMba sUcane). 
\num{6} (biVdi, naDuvaNa dUra, \mo vugaLa) Ace; A badi: \eng{take this over to the post-office} idanunx A badiya aMce kaceVrige tegedukoMDu hoVgu. \eng{asked him over} (dUravalalxda UriniMda yA sathxLadiMda BeVTi \mo vugaLigAgi) bA eMdu avananunx karede, baraheVLide. \eng{he is over in America} avanu deVshadiMdAce yA dUrada amerikadalilxdAdxne. \eng{I am going over to America} nAnu namamx deVshadiMdAce, amerikakekx hoVgutitxdedxVne.

\num{8} ati; adhikavAgi; mitimiVri; ucitavAdudakikxMta yA apeVkiSxtavAgiruvudakikxMta hecAcxgi. \eng{over-anxious} ati kaLavaLadiMda kUDida. \eng{not over well} aSeTxVnU AroVgayxvilalx; aMtha AroVgayxveVnU ilalx. 
\num{9} -kekx savxlapx miVri, tusu hecAcxgi: \eng{I shall have something over} (nananx agatayx kaLedu) savxlapx uLiyutatxde. \eng{20} \eng{kgs and over} ipapxtutx kiloVgArxmf miVri; ipapxtutx kiloVgArxmfgiMta savxlapx hecAcxgi. 
\num{10} modaliniMda koneyavaregU; AdayxMta(vAgi); AmUlAgarxvAgi: \eng{read over} AmUlAgarxvAgi Odu. \eng{count over} AdayxMtavAgi eNisu. \eng{I did it six times over} nAnu adanunx modaliniMda koneyavaregU Aru sala mADide.

\bentry
\word{over-}
\pron{Ovarf-}
\gl{\pUparx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (utatxrapadakekx visheVSaNavAgi) meVlaNa, horagaNa, meVlatxrada, talekeLagAda, adhika, migilAda, meVlina sAthxnakekx yA sAthxnadalilx eMba athaRgaLalilx \parx: \eng{overcoat, overlord, overtime.} 
\num{2} (utatxrapadakekx visheVSaNavAgi seVri) nAmapada, guNavAcaka yA kirxyAvisheVSaNagaLanunx rUpisuvalilx: \eng{over-all, over-board.} 
\num{3} kirxyApadagaLige pUvaRpadavAgi seVri halavomemx visheVSAthaR koDuva padagaLanunx rUpisuvalilx: \eng{over-brim, over-come,} 
\num{4} (adhikaraNAthaRgaLalilx kirxyAvisheVSaNavAgi) meVle; upari; mareyAgi; meVlapxdaravAgi; meVliMda keLakekx; UdhavxRmuKavAgi; meVliMda keLakekx; UdhavxRmuKavAgi yA keLagiMda meVlakekx; kaLedu hoVgi; miVri; jotege; alalxde: \eng{overarch, overbear.} 
\num{5} (sakamaRka dhAtuvinoDane kirxyAvisheVSaNavAgi seVri) sAthaRkavAgi yA saPalavAgi, saMpUNaRvAgi eMbathaRgaLalilx \parx : \eng{over-awe.} 
\num{6} (kirxyApada, guNavAcaka, kirxyAvisheVSaNa yA nAmapadagaLige kirxyAvisheVSaNavAgi ilalxve guNavAcakavAgi seVri) apeVkaSxNiVya yA nidiRSaTx parimiti miVri, satAyxMsha miVri, \mo\ athaRgaLalilx: \eng{over-laden, over-work.} 
\num{7} (AtAmxthaRkavAgi \eng{self} eMba kamaRpadavanunx hoMduva ilalxve BUtakaqdaMtavAgi parxyoVgavAguva kirxyApadagaLanunx rUpisuvAga) `atiyAgi mADuvudariMda tanageV keVDuMTumADiko' eMba athaRdalilx: \eng{over-eat, over-sleep.} 
\num{8} (dhAtuvige yA dhAtuvina niSapxtitxge, ilalxve guNavAcakakekx pUvaRpadavAgi seVri) -kikxMta hecAcxgi, adhikavAgi, adhikataravAgi, anapeVkiSxta maTaTxkekx eMba athaRgaLalilx: \eng{overbalance, overdue.} 
\num{9} (akamaRka dhAtuvige pUvaRpadavAgi seVri sakamaRka dhAtuvanunx racisi, ilalxve nAmapadakekx pUvaRpadavAgi seVri sakamaRka dhAtugaLanunx racisuvAga) migilAgi, miVri, atishayavAgi eMba athaRgaLalilx \parx: \eng{overbuild, overcast.} 
\enum
\emng

\eng{overdo it} (\engit{or} \eng{things)} 
\banum
\alnum{a} vipariVta duDi; miti miVri sharxmisu. 
\alnum{b} ati mADu. 
\eanum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{overdoer}
\pron{OvarfDuarf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} ati mADuvavanu. 
\num{2} ati aBinayisuvavanu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{overdone}
\pron{OvarfDanf}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} ati beVyisida; beVyisidudx hecAcxda: \eng{overdone egg} ati beVyisida moTeTx. 
\num{2} atiyAda; atireVkada; vipariVtavAda; parimiti miVrida: \eng{overdone courtesy} ati vinaya. 
\num{3} ati baLalida; baLali beVsatatx: \eng{you seem a bit overdone by your tedious journey} ninanx parxyAsakaravAda parxyANadiMda niVnu savxlapx hecucx baLalidaMtide. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[overflow(1)]{overflow}
\pron{OvarfpholxV}
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (pAterx \mo vu) tuMbi tuLuku. 
\num{2} (tuMbida parxdeVshadiMda janasamudAya viraLa parxdeVshakekx) sathxLAMtaragoLuLx; valase hoVgu; hari: \eng{the crowded population overflowed into the adjoining territory} kikikxrida A jana samudAya pakakxda parxdeVshakekx ukikx sariyitu. 
\num{3} tuMbi hari; ukikx hari; nadi \mo vu nereyiMda tuMbi daDada meVle hari. 
\num{4} (\rUpa) (kaqtajacnxte \mo vugaLiMda) tuMbiru; tuMbi tuLuku: \eng{my heart overflows with gratitude} nananx haqdaya kaqtajacnxteyiMda tuMbi tuLukutitxde. 
\num{5} (karuNe, Pasalu, \mo vugaLa \vi) vipulavAgiru; daMDiyAgiru; samaqdadhxvAgiru. 
\enum
\emng

\gl{\sakirx}

\num{2} tuMbi hariyuva niVru \mo vu: \eng{to carry off the overflow} tuMbi hariyuva niVranunx, darxvavanunx hora sAgisalu. 
\num{3} ati samaqdidhx; atAyxdhikayx; ati hecacxLa: \eng{an overflow of applicants for the job} A hudedxgAgi ajiRdArara ati hecacxLa, parxvAha. 
\num{4} hora (harivige) kaMDi, dAvxra: \eng{the tank is equipped with an overflow } toTiTxge ukukxniVrina kaMDiyoMdanunx odagiside.

\num{3} (rAshirAshiyAgi koDuvudu, keVLuvudu, \mo vugaLiMda) mUkagoLisu; solelxtatxdaMte mADu; bAyimucicxsu; mAteV horaDadaMte mADu: \eng{overwhelm one with presents} rAshirAshi uDugore koTuTx obabxnige mAteV horaDadaMte mADu. \eng{overwhelm someone with questions} parxshenxgaLa surimaLegaredu obabxnanunx solelxtatxdaMte mADu. 
\num{4} (BagAnxvasheVSagaLu \mo vugaLa rAshiya aDiyalilx) hudugisibiDu; hUtu hoVguvaMte mADu: \eng{the lava from the Vesuvius overwhelmed Pompeii} vesuviyasf jAvxlAmuKi uguLida shilArasa pAMpeV nagaravanenxlalx hUtubiTiTxtu. 
\num{5} (edurALiyanunx) soVlisibiDu; uruLisibiDu. 
\num{6} tuLiduhAku; huTaTxDagisu. 
\num{7} haThAtf vinAshakekx oyuyx; haThAtf nAsha mADu. 
\num{8} (vipariVta vayxvahAra \mo vugaLiMda) muLugisu; tananx meVlina hatoVTi kaLedukoLuLxvaMte mADu. 
\num{9} (\pArxparx) soVlisu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\gl{\gu}
\bmng
\bnum

\num{2} tananx; tananxdeV Ada; tanageV vishiSaTxvAda, vilakaSxNavAda: \eng{has a value all its own} adakekx tananxdeV Ada oMdu bele ide. 
\num{3} savxkiVya; tAneV mADikoMDa; savxyaMkaqta: \eng{let them stew in their own juice} avaru mADikoMDadadxnunx avareV anuBavisali. 
\num{4} adaradeV Ada; adaradeV savxrUpada: \eng{loves truth for its own sake} satayxkAkxgiyeV satayxvanunx pirxVtisutAtxne. 
\num{5} (vayxkitxtavxvanunx otitx heVLuvAga) tananx; tananxdeV: \eng{cooks her own meals} tananx aDigeyanunx tAneV mADikoLuLxtAtxLe. \eng{I am my own master} nanage nAneV yajamAna.

\eanum
\emng
